<p><strong>Features</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Use custom controls for the editable</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Pressing <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">Enter</code> commits the input value</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Pressing <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">Esc</code> reverts the value</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Activate edit mode by double-clicking or focusing on the preview text</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Auto-resize input to fit content</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="anatomy" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Anatomy<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#anatomy"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Check the editable anatomy and part names.</p>

<p>Each part includes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code> attribute to help identify them in the DOM.</p>

<h2 id="usage" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Usage<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Import the editable package:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword module">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token keyword module">as</span> editable</span> <span class="token keyword module">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/editable&quot;</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>The editable package exports two key functions:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">machine</code> - Behavior logic for the editable.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">connect</code> - Maps behavior to JSX props and event handlers.</li>
</ul>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>Pass a unique <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">id</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">useMachine</code> so generated element ids stay predictable.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>Then use the framework integration helpers:</p>
<div data-scope="tabs" data-part="root" id="tabs:editable/usage.mdx" data-orientation="horizontal" dir="ltr" class="w_full max-w_768px bd-w_1px my_8 bg_bg.code.block bdr_6px"><div data-scope="tabs" <h3 id="setting-the-initial-value" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Setting the initial value<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#setting-the-initial-value"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultValue</code> to define the initial value.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>editable<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">defaultValue</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Hello World&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="controlled-value" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Controlled value<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#controlled-value"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">value</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onValueChange</code> to control the value externally.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>editable<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  value<span class="token punctuation">,</span>

</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token function">setValue</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">value</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="controlled-edit-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Controlled edit state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#controlled-edit-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">edit</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onEditChange</code> to control whether the field is in edit mode.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>editable<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token function">setEdit</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">edit</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="listening-for-value-changes" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Listening for value changes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#listening-for-value-changes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Editable supports two ways of listening for value changes:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onValueChange</code>: called when value changes.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onValueCommit</code>: called when the value is committed.</li>
</ul>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>editable<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token function">onValueChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

<h3 id="listening-for-revert-events" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Listening for revert events<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#listening-for-revert-events"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onValueRevert</code> to react when a user cancels editing.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>editable<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

<h3 id="using-custom-controls" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Using custom controls<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#using-custom-controls"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>In some cases, you might need to use custom controls to toggle the edit and read
mode. We use the render prop pattern to provide access to the internal state of
the component.</p>

</span></span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token script"><span class="token language-javascript"></span></span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>script</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>div</span> <span class="token language-javascript"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getRootProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>div</span> <span class="token language-javascript"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getAreaProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>input</span> <span class="token language-javascript"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getInputProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span> <span class="token punctuation">/&gt;</span></span>

</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>div</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>div</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token language-javascript"><span class="token punctuation">{</span>#<span class="token keyword control-flow">if</span> <span class="token operator">!</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">editing</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span>
</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>button</span> <span class="token language-javascript"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getEditTriggerProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>Edit<span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>button</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>

</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>div</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</span><span class="code-line">        <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>button</span> <span class="token language-javascript"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getSubmitTriggerProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>Save<span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>button</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>

</span></div></pre><button type="button" class="px_2 py_1 gap_1 bd-w_1px pos_absolute right_5 top_3 d_flex ai_center fs_xs bg_bg.subtle bd-c_border.subtle cursor_pointer hover:bg_bg.muted"><svg stroke="currentColor" fill="none" stroke-width="2" viewBox="0 0 24 24" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="w_1em h_1em va_middle" height="1em" width="1em" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M8 5H6a2 2 0 00-2 2v12a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2v-1M8 5a2 2 0 002 2h2a2 2 0 002-2M8 5a2 2 0 012-2h2a2 2 0 012 2m0 0h2a2 2 0 012 2v3m2 4H10m0 0l3-3m-3 3l3 3"></path></svg><span>Copy</span></button></div></div></div>
<h3 id="auto-resizing" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Auto-resizing<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#auto-resizing"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">autoResize</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">true</code> to auto-grow the editable as content changes.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>editable<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">autoResize</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>When using autoresize, the input and preview elements should not have any
styles. Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">all: unset</code> if needed and pass any styles to the &quot;area&quot; element
since it&#x27;s shared by the input and preview elements.</p>
<h3 id="setting-a-maxwidth" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Setting a maxWidth<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#setting-a-maxwidth"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>It is common to set a max width when auto-resizing.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>editable<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">autoResize</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">maxWidth</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;320px&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>When the editable reaches the specified max-width, it&#x27;ll clip the preview text
with an ellipsis.</p>
<h3 id="editing-with-double-click" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Editing with double click<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#editing-with-double-click"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The editable supports two modes of activating the &quot;edit&quot; state:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">when the preview part is focused (with pointer or keyboard).</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">when the preview part is double-clicked.</li>
</ul>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">activationMode</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">&quot;dblclick&quot;</code> to only enter edit mode on double click.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>editable<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">activationMode</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;dblclick&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="customizing-submit-behavior" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Customizing submit behavior<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#customizing-submit-behavior"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">submitMode</code> to control when edits are committed.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>editable<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">submitMode</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;enter&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token comment">// &quot;enter&quot; | &quot;blur&quot; | &quot;both&quot; | &quot;none&quot;</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="usage-with-textarea" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Usage with Textarea<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage-with-textarea"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Editable supports using a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">textarea</code> instead of an <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">input</code> field. When a
textarea is used, the editable will commit the value on <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">Cmd + Enter</code> or
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">Ctrl + Enter</code>.</p>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api.getInputProps()</code> to spread input props to the textarea. You might
need to cast the input props to the correct type.</p>
</blockquote>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>textarea</span>
</span></span><span class="code-line highlight-line"><span class="token tag">  <span class="token attr-name">{...(api.getInputProps()</span> <span class="token attr-name">as</span> <span class="token attr-name">HTMLTextareaProps&lt;HTMLTextareaElement</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span><span class="token attr-name">)}</span>
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">/&gt;</span></span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="customizing-placeholder-text" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Customizing placeholder text<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#customizing-placeholder-text"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">placeholder</code> as a string or per-mode object.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>editable<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">placeholder</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token literal-property property">preview</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Click to edit&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token literal-property property">edit</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Type a value&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="customizing-accessibility-labels" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Customizing accessibility labels<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#customizing-accessibility-labels"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">translations</code> to customize control labels.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>editable<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">translations</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token literal-property property">edit</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Edit value&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token literal-property property">submit</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Save&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token literal-property property">cancel</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Cancel&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token literal-property property">input</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Editable input&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="submitting-with-an-external-form" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Submitting with an external form<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#submitting-with-an-external-form"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">form</code> if the hidden input should submit with a form outside the current DOM
subtree.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>editable<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">name</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;value&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">form</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;checkout-form&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="styling-guide" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Styling guide<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#styling-guide"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Each part includes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code> attribute you can target in CSS.</p>
<h3 id="focused-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Focused state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#focused-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the editable is in the focused mode, we set a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-focus</code> attribute on the
&quot;area&quot; part.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;area&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-focus</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* CSS for the editable&#x27;s focus state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="empty-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Empty state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#empty-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the editable&#x27;s value is empty, we set a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-empty</code> attribute on the
&quot;area&quot; part.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;area&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-empty</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* CSS for the editable&#x27;s focus state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="disabled-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Disabled state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#disabled-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the editable is disabled, we set a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-disabled</code> attribute on the &quot;area&quot;
part.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;area&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-disabled</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* CSS for the editable&#x27;s focus state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="methods-and-properties" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Methods and Properties<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#methods-and-properties"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<h3 id="machine-context" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine Context<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The editable machine exposes the following context properties:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">ids</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">Partial&lt;{ root: string; area: string; label: string; preview: string; input: string; control: string; submitTrigger: string; cancelTrigger: string; editTrigger: string; }&gt;</code><span class="d_block">The ids of the elements in the editable. Useful for composition.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">invalid</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the input&#x27;s value is invalid.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">name</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The name attribute of the editable component. Used for form submission.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">form</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The associate form of the underlying input.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">autoResize</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the editable should auto-resize to fit the content.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">activationMode</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">ActivationMode</code><span class="d_block">The activation mode for the preview element.

- &quot;focus&quot; - Enter edit mode when the preview is focused
- &quot;dblclick&quot; - Enter edit mode when the preview is double-clicked
- &quot;click&quot; - Enter edit mode when the preview is clicked
- &quot;none&quot; - Edit can be triggered programmatically only</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">submitMode</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">SubmitMode</code><span class="d_block">The action that triggers submit in the edit mode:

- &quot;enter&quot; - Trigger submit when the enter key is pressed
- &quot;blur&quot; - Trigger submit when the editable is blurred
- &quot;none&quot; - No action will trigger submit. You need to use the submit button
- &quot;both&quot; - Pressing `Enter` and blurring the input will trigger submit</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">selectOnFocus</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether to select the text in the input when it is focused.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">edit</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the editable is in edit mode.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultEdit</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the editable is in edit mode by default.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onEditChange</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: EditChangeDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function to call when the edit mode changes.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">maxLength</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The maximum number of characters allowed in the editable</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">disabled</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the editable is disabled.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">readOnly</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the editable is read-only.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">required</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the editable is required.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">placeholder</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string | { edit: string; preview: string; }</code><span class="d_block">The placeholder text for the editable.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">translations</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">IntlTranslations</code><span class="d_block">The translations for the editable.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">finalFocusEl</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">() =&gt; HTMLElement</code><span class="d_block">The element to receive focus when the editable is closed.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">value</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The controlled value of the editable.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The initial value of the editable when rendered.
Use when you don&#x27;t need to control the value of the editable.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onValueChange</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: ValueChangeDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function to call when the value changes.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onValueRevert</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: ValueChangeDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function to call when the value is reverted.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onValueCommit</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: ValueChangeDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function to call when the value is committed.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">dir</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">&quot;ltr&quot; | &quot;rtl&quot;</code><span class="d_block">The document&#x27;s text/writing direction.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">id</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The unique identifier of the machine.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getRootNode</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">() =&gt; Node | ShadowRoot | Document</code><span class="d_block">A root node to correctly resolve document in custom environments. E.x.: Iframes, Electron.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onPointerDownOutside</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(event: PointerDownOutsideEvent) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when the pointer is pressed down outside the component</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onFocusOutside</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(event: FocusOutsideEvent) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when the focus is moved outside the component</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onInteractOutside</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(event: InteractOutsideEvent) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when an interaction happens outside the component</span></li></ul>
<h3 id="machine-api" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine API<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-api"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The editable <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api</code> exposes the following methods:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">editing</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the editable is in edit mode</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">empty</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the editable value is empty</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">value</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The current value of the editable</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">valueText</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The current value of the editable, or the placeholder if the value is empty</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">setValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(value: string) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function to set the value of the editable</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">clearValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">VoidFunction</code><span class="d_block">Function to clear the value of the editable</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">edit</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">VoidFunction</code><span class="d_block">Function to enter edit mode</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">cancel</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">VoidFunction</code><span class="d_block">Function to exit edit mode, and discard any changes</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">submit</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">VoidFunction</code><span class="d_block">Function to exit edit mode, and submit any changes</span></li></ul>
<h3 id="data-attributes" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Data Attributes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#data-attributes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_8px pl_0! li-t_none li-pos_inside dvd-y_1px"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_4 py_4"><div class="fw_semibold">Area</div><div class="d_flex flex-d_column class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">data-part</kbd></div><span>area</span></div><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">data-focus</kbd></div><span>Present when focused</span></div><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">data-disabled</kbd></div><span>Present when disabled</span></div><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em changes:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eonValueChange\u003c/code\u003e: called when value changes.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eonValueCommit\u003c/code\u003e: called when the value is committed.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode {\n  onValueRevert(details) {\n    console.log(\"Value reverted\", details.value)\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eUsing custom controls\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eIn some cases, you might need to use custom controls to toggle the edit and read\nmode. We use the render prop pattern to provide access to the internal state of\nthe component.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"editable/custom-controls.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eAuto-resizing\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eSet \u003ccode\u003eautoResize\u003c/code\u003e to \u003ccode\u003etrue\u003c/code\u003e to auto-grow the editable as content changes.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(editable.machine, {\n  autoResize: true,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen using autoresize, the input and preview elements should not have any\nstyles. Use \u003ccode\u003eall: unset\u003c/code\u003e if needed and pass any styles to the \"area\" element\nsince it's shared by the input and preview elements.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eSetting a maxWidth\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eIt is common to set a max width when auto-resizing.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2-3}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(editable.machine, {\n  autoResize: true,\n  maxWidth: \"320px\",\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen the editable reaches the specified max-width, it'll clip the preview text\nwith an ellipsis.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eEditing with double click\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe editable supports two modes of activating the \"edit\" state:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003ewhen the preview part is focused (with pointer or keyboard).\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003ewhen the preview part is double-clicked.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eSet \u003ccode\u003eactivationMode\u003c/code\u003e to \u003ccode\u003e\"dblclick\"\u003c/code\u003e to only enter edit mode on double click.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(editable.machine, {\n  activationMode: \"dblclick\",\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eCustomizing submit behavior\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003esubmitMode\u003c/code\u003e to control when edits are committed.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(editable.machine, {\n  submitMode: \"enter\", // \"enter\" | \"blur\" | \"both\" | \"none\"\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eUsage with Textarea\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eEditable supports using a \u003ccode\u003etextarea\u003c/code\u003e instead of an \u003ccode\u003einput\u003c/code\u003e field. When a\ntextarea is used, the editable will commit the value on \u003ccode\u003eCmd + Enter\u003c/code\u003e or\n\u003ccode\u003eCtrl + Enter\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003eapi.getInputProps()\u003c/code\u003e to spread input props to the textarea. {...(api.getInputProps() as HTMLTextareaProps\u0026#x3C;HTMLTextareaElement\u003e)}\n/\u003e\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eCustomizing placeholder line of text. It renders as\nstatic text and transforms into a text input field when the edit interaction is\ntriggered (click, focus, or double-click).\n\n\u003cResources pkg=\"@zag-js/editable\" /\u003e\n\n\u003cShowcase id=\"Editable\" /\u003e\n\n**Features**\n\n- Use custom controls for the editable\n- Pressing `Enter` commits the input value\n- Pressing `Esc` reverts the value\n- Activate edit mode by double-clicking or focusing on the preview text\n- Auto-resize input to fit content\n\n## Installation\n\nInstall the editable package:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"editable/installation.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n## Anatomy\n\nCheck the editable anatomy and part names.\n\n\u003e Each part includes a `data-part` attribute to help identify them in the DOM.\n\n\u003cAnatomy id=\"editable\" /\u003e\n\n## Usage\n\nImport the editable package:\n\n```jsx\nimport * as editable from \"@zag-js/editable\"\n```\n\nThe editable package exports two key functions:\n\n- `machine` - Behavior logic for the editable.\n- `connect` - Maps behavior to JSX props and event handlers.\n\n\u003e Pass a unique `id` to `useMachine` so generated element ids stay predictable.\n\nThen use the framework integration helpers:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"editable/usage.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n### Setting the initial value\n\nSet `defaultValue` to define the initial value.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(editable.machine, {\n  defaultValue: \"Hello World\",\n})\n```\n\n### Controlled value\n\nUse `value` and `onValueChange` to control the value externally.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(editable.machine, {\n  value,\n  onValueChange(details) {\n    setValue(details.value)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Controlled edit state\n\nUse `edit` and `onEditChange` to control whether the field is in edit mode.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(editable.machine, {\n  edit,\n  onEditChange(details) {\n    setEdit(details.edit)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Listening for value changes\n\nEditable supports two ways of listening for value changes:\n\n- `onValueChange`: called when value changes.\n- `onValueCommit`: called when the value is committed.\n\n```jsx {2-4}\nconst service = useMachine(editable.machine, {\n  onValueChange(details) {\n    console.log(\"Value changed\", details.value)\n  },\n  onValueCommit(details) {\n    console.log(\"Value submitted\", details.value)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Listening for revert events\n\nUse `onValueRevert` to react when a user cancels editing.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(editable.machine, {\n  onValueRevert(details) {\n    console.log(\"Value reverted\", details.value)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Using custom controls\n\nIn some cases, you might need to use custom controls to toggle the edit and read\nmode. We use the render prop pattern to provide access to the internal state of\nthe component.\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"editable/custom-controls.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n### Auto-resizing\n\nSet `autoResize` to `true` to auto-grow the editable as content changes.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(editable.machine, {\n  autoResize: true,\n})\n```\n\nWhen using autoresize, the input and preview elements should not have any\nstyles. Use `all: unset` if needed and pass any styles to the \"area\" element\nsince it's shared by the input and preview elements.\n\n### Setting a maxWidth\n\nIt is common to set a max width when auto-resizing.\n\n```jsx {2-3}\nconst service = useMachine(editable.machine, {\n  autoResize: true,\n  maxWidth: \"320px\",\n})\n```\n\nWhen the editable reaches the specified max-width, it'll clip the preview text\nwith an ellipsis.\n\n### Editing with double click\n\nThe editable supports two modes of activating the \"edit\" state:\n\n- when the preview part is focused (with pointer or keyboard).\n- when the preview part is double-clicked.\n\nSet `activationMode` to `\"dblclick\"` to only enter edit mode on double click.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(editable.machine, {\n  activationMode: \"dblclick\",\n})\n```\n\n### Customizing submit behavior\n\nUse `submitMode` to control when edits are committed.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(editable.machine, {\n  submitMode: \"enter\", // \"enter\" | \"blur\" | \"both\" | \"none\"\n})\n```\n\n### Usage with Textarea\n\nEditable supports using a `textarea` instead of an `input` field. When a\ntextarea is used, the editable will commit the value on `Cmd + Enter` or\n`Ctrl + Enter`.\n\n\u003e Use `api.getInputProps()` to spread input props to the textarea. You might\n\u003e need to cast the input props to the correct type.\n\n```tsx {2}\n\u003ctextarea\n  {...(api.getInputProps() as HTMLTextareaProps\u003cHTMLTextareaElement\u003e)}\n/\u003e\n```\n\n### Customizing placeholder text\n\nSet `placeholder` as a string or per-mode object.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(editable.machine, {\n  placeholder: {\n    preview: \"Click to edit\",\n    edit: \"Type a value\",\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Customizing accessibility labels\n\nUse `translations` to customize control labels.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(editable.machine, {\n  translations: {\n    edit: \"Edit value\",\n    submit: \"Save\",\n    cancel: \"Cancel\",\n    input: \"Editable input\",\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Submitting with an external form\n\nSet `form` if the hidden input should submit with a form outside the current DOM\nsubtree.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(editable.machine, {\n  name: \"value\",\n  form: \"checkout-form\",\n})\n```\n\n## Styling guide\n\nEach part includes a `data-part` attribute you can target in CSS.\n\n### Focused state\n\nWhen the editable is in the focused mode, we set a `data-focus` attribute on the\n\"area\" part.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"area\"][data-focus] {\n  /* CSS for the editable's focus state */\n}\n```\n\n### Empty state\n\nWhen the editable's value is empty, we set a `data-empty` attribute on the\n\"area\" part.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"area\"][data-empty] {\n  /* CSS for the editable's focus state */\n}\n```\n\n### Disabled state\n\nWhen the editable is disabled, we set a `data-disabled` attribute on the \"area\"\npart.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"area\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* CSS for the editable's focus state */\n}\n```\n\n## Methods and Properties\n\n### Machine Context\n\nThe editable machine exposes the following context properties:\n\n\u003cContextTable name=\"editable\" /\u003e\n\n### Machine API\n\nThe editable `api` exposes the following methods:\n\n\u003cApiTable name=\"editable\" /\u003e\n\n### Data Attributes\n\n\u003cDataAttrTable name=\"editable\" /\u003e\n\n## Accessibility\n\n### Keyboard Interactions\n\n\u003cKeyboardTable name=\"editable\" /\u003e"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"5:[\"$\",\"$Le\",null,{\"doc\":{\"title\":\"Editable\",\"description\":\"Using the editable machine in your
